    "### 1Ô∏è‚É£ Lakukan agregasi\n", 
    "\n", 
    "* Kelompokkan data berdasarkan metode pembayaran dan gunakan fungsi agregasi menghitung rataan (mean)\n", 
    "* Assign ke dalam sebuah variabel\n", 
    "* Urutkan nilainya dari yang terbesar hingga ke yang terkecil\n", 
    "* Tampilkan data hasil agregasi"

   "source": [ 
    "# Proses agregasi data\n", 
    "avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod = data_custchurn.groupby(['paymentmethod'], as_index = False)\\\n", 
    "                                                     .agg(avg_monthly_charges = ('monthlycharges', 'mean'))\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Bulatkan menjadi 2 angka dibelakang koma\n", 
    "avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod['avg_monthly_charges'] = avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod['avg_monthly_charges'].round(2)\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Urutkan data\n", 
    "avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod = avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod.sort_values(\n", 
    "    by = 'avg_monthly_charges',\n", 
    "    ascending = False,\n", 
    "    ignore_index = True\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Tampilkan data hasil agregasi\n", 
    "display(avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod)"

    "### 3Ô∏è‚É£ Re-design Plot\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Agar lebih advance dari sisi penampilan teman2 bisa melakukan hal berikut"

   "cell_type": "code", 
   "source": [ 
    "# Import library yang dibutuhkan\n", 
    "import seaborn as sns\n", 
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Atur ukuran grafik\n", 
    "plt.figure(\n", 
    "    figsize = (6, 4)\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Inisialisasi grafik\n", 
    "sns.barplot(\n", 
    "    data = avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod,\n", 
    "    x = 'avg_monthly_charges',\n", 
    "    y = 'paymentmethod',\n", 
    "    orient = 'h'\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Mencari nilai tertinggi\n", 
    "max_value = max(avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod['avg_monthly_charges'])\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Memberikan warna biru tua pada data tertinggi dan biru muda pada data selainnya\n", 
    "for i, v in enumerate(avg_monthlycharges_per_paymentmethod['avg_monthly_charges']):\n", 
    "    if v == max_value:\n", 
    "        set_color = '#0C356A'      # Hex Warna biru tua\n", 
    "    else:\n", 
    "        set_color = '#279EFF'      # Hex Warna biru muda\n", 
    "\n", 
    "    plt.text(\n", 
    "        v + 0.5,\n", 
    "        i,\n", 
    "        str(v),\n", 
    "        color = set_color,\n", 
    "        fontweight = 'light'\n", 
    "    )\n", 
    "\n", 
    "    plt.gca().get_children()[i].set_color(set_color)\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Menambahkan judul\n", 
    "plt.title(\n", 
    "    label = 'Rataan Monthly Charges Berdasarkan Metode Pembayaran' ,\n", 
    "    x = 0.35,\n", 
    "    pad = 35,\n", 
    "    fontsize = 15,\n", 
    "    fontweight = 'bold'\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "plt.suptitle(\n", 
    "    t = f'Electronic Check menjadi Metode Pembayaran dengan Rataan Monthly Charges tertinggi sebesar ${max_value}',\n", 
    "    x = 0.31,\n", 
    "    y = 0.98,\n", 
    "    fontsize = 8,\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Mengatur xlabel dan ylabel\n", 
    "plt.ylabel('')\n", 
    "plt.xlabel('Avg. Monthly Charges')\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Menghapus tepian\n", 
    "sns.despine()\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Tampilkan grafik\n", 
    "plt.show()" 
   ],

    "### 1Ô∏è‚É£ Menambah kolom baru\n", 
    "\n", 
    "* Pada contoh proses pengkategorian ini akan digunakan numpy.select sehingga perlu mengimpor library numpy terlebih dahulu\n", 
    "* Buat variabel bertipe list beri nama conditions yang memuat kondisi yang harus dipenuhi\n", 
    "* Buat variabel bertipe list beri nama values yang memuat kriteria kondisi\n", 
    "* Pada DataFrame `data_custchurn`, tambahkan satu kolom baru misalkan dinamai <b>tenure_category</b> lalu lakukan pengkondisian pada DataFrame\n", 
    "* Tampilkan datanya (kolom customerid, tenure dan tenure_category saja) untuk memastikan <br><br>\n", 
    "\n", 
    "*referensi : https://towardsdatascience.com/creating-conditional-columns-on-pandas-with-numpy-select-and-where-methods-8ee6e2dbd5d5*" 
   ], 
   "metadata": { 
    "id": "MsYyKz8j4kvY" 
   } 
  }, 
  { 
   "cell_type": "code", 
   "source": [ 
    "# Import library yang dibutuhkan\n", 
    "import numpy as np\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Menentukan kondisi dan nilai terkait\n", 
    "conditions = [\n", 
    "    (data_custchurn['tenure'] < 21),\n", 
    "    (data_custchurn['tenure'] >= 21) & (data_custchurn['tenure'] <= 40),\n", 
    "    (data_custchurn['tenure'] > 40)\n", 
    "]\n", 
    "\n", 
    "values = ['Low', 'Medium', 'High']\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Mengkategorikan data tenure berdasarkan kondisi tertentu dengan np.select()\n", 
    "data_custchurn['tenure_category'] = np.select(\n", 
    "    conditions,\n", 
    "    values,\n", 
    "    default = 'unknown'\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Menampilkan DataFrame\n", 
    "display(data_custchurn)"

    "### 2Ô∏è‚É£ Lakukan Agregasi\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Setelah diperoleh kolom baru, lakukan proses agregasi data dengan menghitung banyak data per masing-masing kategori tenurenya (tenure_category). Untuk melakukan hal ini kalian bisa melakukan hitung banyak data unik (nunique) pada kolom customerid lalu kelompokan berdasarkan tenure_category. Lalu urutkan berdasarkan total customer tiap kategori" 
   ], 
   "metadata": { 
    "id": "qz-I0avi6gNW" 
   } 
  }, 
  { 
   "cell_type": "code", 
   "source": [ 
    "# Proses agregasi data\n", 
    "countdata_per_tenurecategory = data_custchurn.groupby('tenure_category')['customerid'].nunique().reset_index()\n", 
    "countdata_per_tenurecategory.columns = ['tenure_category', 'total_customer']\n", 
    "# Urutkan data\n", 
    "countdata_per_tenurecategory = countdata_per_tenurecategory.sort_values(\n", 
    "    by='total_customer',\n", 
    "    ascending=False,\n", 
    "    ignore_index=True\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Tampilkan data hasil agregasi\n", 
    "display(countdata_per_tenurecategory)" 
   ],

    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "plt.axis('equal')\n", 
    "\n",

    "# Import library yang dibutuhkan\n", 
    "import seaborn as sns\n", 
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Atur ukuran figure grafik\n", 
    "plt.figure(\n", 
    "    figsize = (8, 6)\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Inisialisasi variabel sebagai label dan data hitung\n", 
    "total_customer = countdata_per_tenurecategory['total_customer']\n", 
    "customer_category = countdata_per_tenurecategory['tenure_category']\n", 
    "\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Hitung total datanya (sum total_customer)\n", 
    "sum_customer = total_customer.sum()\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Inisialisasi nilai pada grafik pie\n", 
    "plt.pie(\n", 
    "    x = total_customer ,\n", 
    "    labels = customer_category,\n", 
    "    autopct = lambda pct: f'{pct:.1f}%\\n({int(pct/100*sum_customer)})',\n", 
    "    startangle = 90,\n", 
    "    explode = (0, 0, 0.02),\n", 
    "    colors = ['#efbbff', '#be29ec', '#800080']\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Beri Judul\n", 
    "plt.title(\n", 
    "    label = 'Total Customer Per Kategori Tenure',\n", 
    "    pad = 40,\n", 
    "    fontsize = 15,\n", 
    "    fontweight = 'bold'\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Beri suptitle (sub judul)\n", 
    "plt.suptitle(\n", 
    "    t = 'Kategori = Low {<21) | Medium {21-40} | High {>40}',\n", 
    "    x = 0.5,\n", 
    "    y = 0.92,\n", 
    "    fontsize = 10,\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Menampilkan diagram pie\n", 
    "plt.show()"

    "import math\n", 
    "import seaborn as sns\n", 
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Assuming data_custchurn['totalcharges'] has been processed as per the previous steps\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Set the figure size\n", 
    "plt.figure(figsize=(8, 6))\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Initialize the data for histogram\n", 
    "data_hist = data_custchurn['totalcharges']\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Calculate number of bins using Sturges' formula\n", 
    "num_bins = 1 + int(round(math.log2(len(data_hist))))\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Create a histogram\n", 
    "sns.histplot(\n", 
    "    data_hist,\n", 
    "    bins=num_bins,\n", 
    "    color='#D3D04F'\n", 
    ")\n", 
    "\n", 
    "# Add title\n", 
    "plt.title(\n", 
    "    label='Distribusi Total Charges Customers',\n", 
    "    pad = 40,\n", 
    "    fontsize = 15,\n", 
    "    fontweight = 'bold'\n", 
    ")\n",
